Hygiene: When I first entered the bathroom in the room, I smelled a smell of air freshener + urine. The pictures of the sheets and quilt were all real shots. After taking a shower and getting ready to go to bed, I realized that they looked really dirty. Although the staff explained that the sheets had been changed, it was really uncomfortable if they were not cleaned properly. . .
Facilities: The central air conditioning in the room is very powerful and deserves praise! However, the Internet speed is very slow. If you want to use your mobile phone to cast the screen to watch videos, it will basically be one lag after another. Also, the bed is actually very far away from the TV, and the TV is placed in the corner. Sitting on the sofa and watching it will be blocked by the cabinet decorations.
2 free tickets to the Laojun Cave Scenic Area: The hotel has a strong geographical advantage and is very close to the scenic area. Thank you very much for the free tickets~
Breakfast: The breakfast buffet is okay and quite rich.
In short, I sincerely hope that the hotel can strengthen its hygiene management.
